[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring an interactive libFuzzer run against the XML2 API fuzz target, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer detected a double-free error. The failure occurs in the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` function of `libxml2/fuzz/api.c` when fuzzing comment-node[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPIs. A single [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m-byte buffer is freed twice, triggering an abort.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  A memory management error: AddressSanitizer reports an “attempting double-free” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the fuzz target’s test callback.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What happens  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `api.c`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Inside that function, a comment node is created and its text is duplicated via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlStrdup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich uses `xmlFuzzMalloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. That allocated buffer is freed once as part of the comment-node teardown.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Later in the same test iteration, the same pointer is freed again, leading to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man abort triggered by AddressSanitizer.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The backtrace pinpoints the first free at line [0m[1;36m3580[0m[39m of `api.c` in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The allocation path runs through `xmlFuzzMalloc` → `xmlStrndup` → [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlNewComment`.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The double-free is detected at `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `asan_malloc_linux.cpp`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Only a single input is processed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe fuzzer was configured with `-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the error reproduces immediately on `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to inspect  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `libxml2/fuzz/api.c`, especially around the `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation at line [0m[1;36m3580[0m[39m.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Memory allocation wrappers in `libxml2/fuzz/fuzz.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `xmlFuzzMalloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • String duplication routines in `libxml2/xmlstring.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlStrndup`, [0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz/api.[0m[1;92mc:1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m200[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m: * api.c: a libFuzzer target to test node-related API functions.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m: * See Copyright for the status of this software.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m: * This is a simple virtual machine which runs fuzz data as a program.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m: * An important design goal is to execute as many API calls as possible[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m: * per input byte.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m: * We use a fixed number of registers for basic types like integers[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m11[0m[39m: * or strings as well as libxml2 objects like xmlNode. The opcodes are[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m12[0m[39m: * single bytes which typically result in a call to an API function[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m13[0m[39m: * using the freshest registers for each argument type and storing the[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m14[0m[39m: * result in the stalest register. This can be implemented using a ring[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m15[0m[39m: * buffer.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m17[0m[39m: * There are a few other opcodes to initialize or duplicate registers,[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m18[0m[39m: * so all kinds of API calls can potentially be generated from fuzz[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m: * data.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m: * This architecture is similar to stack machine and benefits from[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m: * great code density. The main difference is that values aren't[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m: * destroyed when popping arguments from the stack and that the bottom[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m: * of the stack is eventually overwritten if the ring buffer overflows.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m: * The main complication is memory management of nodes. Whenever a[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m: * reference between two nodes is removed, whether by an API call or[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m: * the VM clearing a register, we must check whether this leaves[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m: * unreferenced nodes which can then be freed. There are no opcodes[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m: * to free a node explicitly. The FIFO patterns generated by[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * overflowing the ring buffer and freeing the registers at the end of[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m: * a program seem to do a good enough job.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:#include <stdlib.h>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:#include <string.h>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:#define XML_DEPRECATED[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:#include <libxml/catalog.h>[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:#include <libxml/HTMLtree.h>[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:#include <libxml/parser.h>[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:#include <libxml/tree.h>[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:#include <libxml/xmlerror.h>[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:#include [0m[32m"fuzz.h"[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:#if [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:  #define DEBUG printf[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:#else[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:  #define [0m[1;35mDEBUG[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:#define MAX_CONTENT     [0m[1;36m100[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:#define MAX_COPY_NODES   [0m[1;36m50[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:#define MAX_COPY_OPS     [0m[1;36m20[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:typedef enum [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Basic operations *[0m[35m/[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    OP_CREATE_INTEGER,[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:    OP_CREATE_STRING,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:    OP_DUP_INTEGER,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    OP_DUP_STRING,[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    OP_DUP_NODE,[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m*** tree.h ***[0m[35m/[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3563[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3570[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3571[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3573[0m[39m:                break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3574[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3575[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3576[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxmlFuzzCheckFailureReport[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->opName, oomReport, ioReport[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3577[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3578[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3579[0m[39m:    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3580[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3581[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3582[0m[39m:    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3583[0m[39m:        xmlNodePtr node = vars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3584[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3585[0m[39m:        vars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3586[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mdropNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3587[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3588[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3589[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlFuzzInjectFailure[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3590[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlFuzzDataCleanup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3591[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlResetLastError[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3592[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3593[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3594[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify the root cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The AddressSanitizer report shows that the [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m‐byte buffer allocated by xmlStrdup[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39minside xmlNewComment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is being freed twice at the end of each fuzz-target [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvocation.  Both frees occur in the harness’s string-cleanup loop:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The only way the same pointer can appear twice in vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m is if the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness places the comment’s internal content pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe xmlStrdup’d buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits string registers—so that the harness frees it—and the library also frees it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen dropping the node.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Tracing the code reveals the culprit: the OP_XML_NODE_[0m[1;33mGET[0m[39m_CONTENT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand similar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcases in the fuzzer loop invoke xmlNodeGetContent [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor xmlNodeGetRawContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen store the returned pointer in vars->strings via setStr.  For a comment node, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlNodeGetContent returns node->content directly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno duplication[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the harness [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstores the node’s own content pointer.  That pointer is later freed both by the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary [0m[1;39m([0m[39mduring [0m[1;35mdropNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and by [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediate double-free on the very next iteration.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing behavior except for safe memory handling  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to test xmlNodeGetContent and related APIs in the harness, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut we must not blindly stash the returned pointer into the string register for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlater free.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Instead, whenever we call an API that returns an internal pointer owned by the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. xmlNodeGetContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, we must duplicate it before registering it in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, so that:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • The harness owns and frees only its private copy.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • The library retains ownership of its internal buffer and frees it via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdropNode without conflict.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Concrete patch plan [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto apply on the initial codebase[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate the [0m[1;35mhandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for OP_XML_NODE_[0m[1;33mGET[0m[39m_CONTENT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand any sibling cases that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn an internal string pointer, such as OP_XML_NODE_LIST_[0m[1;33mGET[0m[39m_STRING, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOP_XML_BUF_[0m[1;33mGET[0m[39m_NODE_CONTENT, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in fuzz/api.c, around where the big opcode [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mswitch lives.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Change the code in those cases from:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        const xmlChar *content = [0m[1;35mxmlNodeGetContent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mgetNode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        xmlChar *dup = NULL;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        const xmlChar *content = [0m[1;35mxmlNodeGetContent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mgetNode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            dup = [0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, dup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      That way, dup is a freshly allocated buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mowned by the harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmirrors the API’s output, and setStr will free any prior string in that register [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore storing dup.  The original content pointer remains owned by the library and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis freed exactly once via dropNode.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Repeat this pattern for every opcode that:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Calls a libxml2 function returning an xmlChar* that points to library-owned[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately stores it into the harness’s string registers for later free.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why this fixes the double-free and preserves logic  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By duplicating the API’s returned string, the harness no longer holds a direct[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malias to the library’s internal buffer.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness still frees its own copy in the normal cleanup loop, avoiding a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleak.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The library side still frees its internal buffer when the node/document is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdestroyed, preserving correct ownership semantics.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other fuzz-target behavior—exercising the same APIs, same opcodes—remains [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.  No test or harness logic is removed or disabled.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slightly higher memory usage: Each call to xmlNodeGetContent now allocates an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextra buffer.  However, since inputs are bounded [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe harness already allocated [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthese strings via xmlFuzzMalloc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the doc size is small under fuzzing, this [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverhead is acceptable.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In edge cases where xmlStrdup fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL return[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked; [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe harness’s oomReport logic covers null strings gracefully.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other opcodes depend on the raw library pointer, so no functionality loss.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference to similar pattern in harness  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OP_CREATE_STRING and OP_DUP_STRING already use copyStr + setStr to manage [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness-owned buffers.  We are aligning OP_XML_NODE_[0m[1;33mGET[0m[39m_CONTENT and relatives to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mharness owns the copy, library owns its buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo modifications to the harness’s free loop, to external libraries, or to tests are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired.  This patch strictly confines changes to the API-fuzzer handling of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary-returned strings to enforce correct ownership and eliminate double-free.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
